plane-crazy 2018-10-31 18:06:27 Tuning control surfaces is trial and error if u dont know which way is the "lower" or "raise" side
plane-crazy 2018-10-31 18:07:52 Also tune control surfaces to suit whatever flight controls you are used to (mines GTA San Andreas-style flight controls)
plane-crazy 2018-10-31 18:12:44 As for ailerons:
Tune just one control surface on the left first.
Then press the button you assigned to "roll left".

The control surface should raise. If it lowers, reverse the controls, do a quick test for confirmation, copy and paste it to the other control surfaces on the left wing(s)
Then tune the control surfaces on the right side to the reverse of the tuning you used on the left side.
